## Instruction

I am preparing to open a stock position today. `stock.xlsx` contains the companies I want to purchase and and I plan to buy all the company shares in the form(Alibaba to be bought as a Hong Kong stock, and BYD, Ping An Insurance and Wuxi AppTec as A-shares). Please establish the position according to a 4:3:3 ratio for US stocks, Hong Kong stocks, and A-shares, respectively. My total capital is $1 million USD. Please calculate exchange rates and stock prices based on today's opening prices. Purchases should be made in whole shares, and A-shares must be bought in multiples of 100 shares (one lot). Based on this, please provide me with a position-building plan and fill in the blank spaces in the table with the final position information. Fill the Initial_position_size with numbers only. Please stop there and do not perform any additional actions.

```python 
# Let me create a comprehensive calculation for the position building plan
# First, let me organize all the stock data I've collected

# US Stocks (40% = $400,000)
us_stocks = {
    'Microsoft': {'ticker': 'MSFT', 'price': 517.93, 'open': 510.61},
    'Apple': {'ticker': 'AAPL', 'price': 245.50, 'open': 241.175},
    'NVIDIA': {'ticker': 'NVDA', 'price': 176.67, 'open': 176.1},
    'AMD': {'ticker': 'AMD', 'price': 157.39, 'open': 157.38},
    'Google': {'ticker': 'GOOGL', 'price': 254.72, 'open': 253.26},
    'Meta': {'ticker': 'META', 'price': 778.38, 'open': 787.205}
}

# Hong Kong Stocks (30% = $300,000) - using HKD prices, need to convert
hk_stocks = {
    'Meituan': {'ticker': '3690.HK', 'price_hkd': 106.3, 'open_hkd': 105.6},
    'XIAOMI': {'ticker': '1810.HK', 'price_hkd': 56.7, 'open_hkd': 57.4},
    'Alibaba': {'ticker': '9988.HK', 'price_hkd': 159.1, 'open_hkd': 158.9},
    'Tencent': {'ticker': '0700.HK', 'price_hkd': 642.5, 'open_hkd': 647.0}
}

# Exchange rates (approximate current rates)
usd_to_hkd = 7.8  # 1 USD = 7.8 HKD
usd_to_cny = 7.3   # 1 USD = 7.3 CNY

# Convert HK stock prices to USD using opening prices
for stock in hk_stocks:
    hk_stocks[stock]['price_usd'] = hk_stocks[stock]['open_hkd'] / usd_to_hkd
    hk_stocks[stock]['open_usd'] = hk_stocks[stock]['open_hkd'] / usd_to_hkd

print("US Stocks (using opening prices):")
for name, data in us_stocks.items():
    print(f"{name}: ${data['open']:.2f}")

print(f"\nHong Kong Stocks (converted to USD using opening prices, 1 USD = {usd_to_hkd} HKD):")
for name, data in hk_stocks.items():
    print(f"{name}: HK${data['open_hkd']:.2f} = ${data['open_usd']:.2f}")
```

```python 
# Complete position building calculation
import math

# Total capital
total_capital_usd = 1000000

# Allocation ratios
us_allocation = 0.4  # 40%
hk_allocation = 0.3  # 30%
a_share_allocation = 0.3  # 30%

# Capital per category
us_capital = total_capital_usd * us_allocation  # $400,000
hk_capital = total_capital_usd * hk_allocation  # $300,000
a_share_capital = total_capital_usd * a_share_allocation  # $300,000

print(f"Capital Allocation:")
print(f"US Stocks: ${us_capital:,.0f}")
print(f"Hong Kong Stocks: ${hk_capital:,.0f}")
print(f"A-Shares: ${a_share_capital:,.0f}")
print()

# Exchange rates
usd_to_hkd = 7.8
usd_to_cny = 7.3

# US Stocks data (using opening prices)
us_stocks = {
    'Microsoft': {'ticker': 'MSFT', 'open_price': 510.61},

# A-Share stocks data (using opening prices)

    'Moutai': {'ticker': '600519.SS', 'open_price_cny': 1467.99, 'open_price_usd': 1467.99/usd_to_cny},
    'CATL': {'ticker': '300750.SZ', 'open_price_cny': 325.9, 'open_price_usd': 325.9/usd_to_cny},  # Note: This seems to be the opening price from the data
    'Ping An Insurance': {'ticker': '601318.SS', 'open_price_cny': 55.29, 'open_price_usd': 55.29/usd_to_cny},
    'BYD': {'ticker': '002594.SZ', 'open_price_cny': 106.6, 'open_price_usd': 106.6/usd_to_cny},
    'WuXi AppTec': {'ticker': '603259.SS', 'open_price_cny': 107.7, 'open_price_usd': 107.7/usd_to_cny}
}

print("Stock Opening Prices:")
print("\nUS Stocks:")
for name, data in us_stocks.items():
    print(f"{name}: ${data['open_price']:.2f}")

print(f"\nHong Kong Stocks (1 USD = {usd_to_hkd} HKD):")
for name, data in hk_stocks.items():
    print(f"{name}: HK${data['open_price_hkd']:.2f} = ${data['open_price_usd']:.2f}")

print(f"\nA-Share Stocks (1 USD = {usd_to_cny} CNY):")
for name, data in a_share_stocks.items():
    print(f"{name}: ¬•{data['open_price_cny']:.2f} = ${data['open_price_usd']:.2f}")

print("\n" + "="*80)
print("POSITION BUILDING PLAN")
print("="*80)

# Calculate positions for each category
def calculate_equal_weight_positions(stocks_dict, total_capital, currency_type="USD"):
    num_stocks = len(stocks_dict)
    capital_per_stock = total_capital / num_stocks
    positions = {}
    
    for name, data in stocks_dict.items():
        if currency_type == "USD":
            price_usd = data['open_price']
            shares = int(capital_per_stock / price_usd)  # Whole shares only
            actual_cost = shares * price_usd
        elif currency_type == "HKD":
            price_usd = data['open_price_usd']
            shares = int(capital_per_stock / price_usd)  # Whole shares only
            actual_cost = shares * price_usd
        elif currency_type == "CNY":
            price_usd = data['open_price_usd']
            shares_float = capital_per_stock / price_usd
            # A-shares must be bought in multiples of 100 (one lot)
            shares = int(shares_float / 100) * 100  # Round down to nearest 100
            actual_cost = shares * price_usd
            
        positions[name] = {
            'shares': shares,
            'cost_usd': actual_cost,
            'ticker': data['ticker']
        }
    
    return positions

# Calculate positions
us_positions = calculate_equal_weight_positions(us_stocks, us_capital, "USD")
hk_positions = calculate_equal_weight_positions(hk_stocks, hk_capital, "HKD")
a_share_positions = calculate_equal_weight_positions(a_share_stocks, a_share_capital, "CNY")

# Display results
print(f"\n1. US STOCKS POSITIONS (Target: ${us_capital:,.0f})")
print("-" * 60)
us_total_cost = 0
for name, pos in us_positions.items():
    price = us_stocks[name]['open_price']
    print(f"{name:12} ({pos['ticker']:4}): {pos['shares']:4} shares √ó ${price:7.2f} = ${pos['cost_usd']:8.0f}")
    us_total_cost += pos['cost_usd']
print(f"{'':12} {'':6} {'':15} Total: ${us_total_cost:8.0f}")
print(f"{'':12} {'':6} {'':15} Unused: ${us_capital - us_total_cost:8.0f}")

print(f"\n2. HONG KONG STOCKS POSITIONS (Target: ${hk_capital:,.0f})")
print("-" * 60)
hk_total_cost = 0
for name, pos in hk_positions.items():
    price_hkd = hk_stocks[name]['open_price_hkd']
    price_usd = hk_stocks[name]['open_price_usd']
    print(f"{name:12} ({pos['ticker']:7}): {pos['shares']:4} shares √ó HK${price_hkd:6.2f} = ${pos['cost_usd']:8.0f}")
    hk_total_cost += pos['cost_usd']
print(f"{'':12} {'':9} {'':15} Total: ${hk_total_cost:8.0f}")
print(f"{'':12} {'':9} {'':15} Unused: ${hk_capital - hk_total_cost:8.0f}")

print(f"\n3. A-SHARE POSITIONS (Target: ${a_share_capital:,.0f})")
print("-" * 60)
a_share_total_cost = 0
for name, pos in a_share_positions.items():
    price_cny = a_share_stocks[name]['open_price_cny']
    price_usd = a_share_stocks[name]['open_price_usd']
    lots = pos['shares'] // 100
    print(f"{name:17} ({pos['ticker']:10}): {pos['shares']:4} shares ({lots:2} lots) √ó ¬•{price_cny:7.2f} = ${pos['cost_usd']:8.0f}")
    a_share_total_cost += pos['cost_usd']
print(f"{'':17} {'':12} {'':20} Total: ${a_share_total_cost:8.0f}")
print(f"{'':17} {'':12} {'':20} Unused: ${a_share_capital - a_share_total_cost:8.0f}")

total_invested = us_total_cost + hk_total_cost + a_share_total_cost
total_unused = total_capital_usd - total_invested

print(f"\n" + "="*60)
print(f"SUMMARY")
print(f"="*60)
print(f"Total Capital:     ${total_capital_usd:10,.0f}")
print(f"Total Invested:    ${total_invested:10,.0f}")
print(f"Total Unused:      ${total_unused:10,.0f}")
print(f"Utilization Rate:  {(total_invested/total_capital_usd)*100:8.1f}%")

# Prepare data for Excel update
excel_data = []
all_positions = {**us_positions, **hk_positions, **a_share_positions}

print(f"\n" + "="*60)
print("POSITION DATA FOR EXCEL UPDATE")
print(f"="*60)
for name, pos in all_positions.items():
    print(f"{name}: {pos['shares']} shares")
    excel_data.append((name, pos['shares']))

print(f"\nExchange rates used:")
print(f"1 USD = {usd_to_hkd} HKD")
print(f"1 USD = {usd_to_cny} CNY")
```
</div>

```python 

import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime

# Get today's date in YYYY-MM-DD format
today_date = datetime.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')

stock_list = {
    "Meituan": {"ticker": "3690.HK", "market": "HK"}, "Microsoft": {"ticker": "MSFT", "market": "US"},
    "Moutai": {"ticker": "600519.SS", "market": "A"}, "Apple": {"ticker": "AAPL", "market": "US"},
    "CATL": {"ticker": "300750.SZ", "market": "A"}, "XIAOMI": {"ticker": "1810.HK", "market": "HK"},
    "NVIDIA": {"ticker": "NVDA", "market": "US"}, "Alibaba": {"ticker": "9988.HK", "market": "HK"},
    "Ping An Insurance": {"ticker": "601318.SS", "market": "A"}, "AMD": {"ticker": "AMD", "market": "US"},
    "Wuxi AppTec": {"ticker": "603259.SS", "market": "A"},"Tencent": {"ticker": "0700.HK", "market": "HK"},
    "BYD": {"ticker": "002594.SZ", "market": "A"}, "Google": {"ticker": "GOOGL", "market": "US"},
    "Meta": {"ticker": "META", "market": "US"}
}

usd_hkd_rate = default_api.yahoo_finance_get_stock_price_by_date(ticker="HKD=X", date=today_date)['price']
usd_cny_rate = default_api.yahoo_finance_get_stock_price_by_date(ticker="CNY=X", date=today_date)['price']

capital = 1000000
us_capital = capital * 0.4
hk_capital = capital * 0.3
a_capital = capital * 0.3

us_stocks = {k: v for k, v in stock_list.items() if v['market'] == 'US'}
hk_stocks = {k: v for k, v in stock_list.items() if v['market'] == 'HK'}
a_stocks = {k: v for k, v in stock_list.items() if v['market'] == 'A'}

us_capital_per_stock = us_capital / len(us_stocks)
hk_capital_per_stock = hk_capital / len(hk_stocks)
a_capital_per_stock = a_capital / len(a_stocks)

results = []
for stock, details in stock_list.items():
    price_data = default_api.yahoo_finance_get_stock_price_by_date(ticker=details['ticker'], date=today_date)
    open_price = price_data['price']
    
    if details['market'] == 'US':
        shares = int(us_capital_per_stock / open_price)
    elif details['market'] == 'HK':
        shares = int((hk_capital_per_stock * usd_hkd_rate) / open_price)
    elif details['market'] == 'A':
        shares = int((a_capital_per_stock * usd_cny_rate) / open_price)
        shares = (shares // 100) * 100 # Round down to the nearest 100
        
    results.append([stock, details['ticker'], shares])

default_api.excel_write_data_to_excel(
    filepath="/workspace/dumps/workspace/stock.xlsx",
    sheet_name="Sheet1",
    data=results,
    start_cell="A2"
)

print(results)

```
